The main problem in the cooperativization movement at present is: the policy of voluntary mutual benefit is not fully implemented, and the interests of middle peasants are not paid enough attention to in the aspects of stock investment, horse price, rent, agricultural tools, and manure pricing; on the other hand, there are also some phenomena of excluding poor peasants; in leadership, there is a tendency to emphasize the commune and neglect the group, and the propaganda of the policies and guidelines of the cooperativization movement is not deep enough; some production cooperatives have weak cadres, and some communes have impure leadership. These shortcomings are inseparable from the bureaucracy of the leading organs, which do not understand the situation below and do not give specific instructions on policies and methods, and after the tasks are assigned, there is a lack of in-depth inspection and help, and some rural cadres have poor work styles or low policy level and lack of experience, often only care about completing the tasks and do not know how to educate the masses, resulting in some phenomena of forced orders. We should mainly educate these cadres patiently, improve their policy and ideological level, and help them correct their shortcomings and errors. But we must strictly distinguish between those who have degenerated and committed lawless and disorderly acts, especially counter-revolutionary saboteurs. Some people, due to a lack of vigilance against the tricks of class enemies, cannot distinguish between the shortcomings and deviations of our cadres in their work and the deliberate sabotage of counter-revolutionary elements, and attribute many serious problems in rural areas caused by the sabotage of the enemy to the account of rural cadres, or exaggerate the errors and shortcomings of a few cadres into the errors and shortcomings of the majority of cadres, and do not see the hard work and selfless dedication of our broad grassroots cadres, which is obviously incorrect.

The supervisory organs at all levels have suggested that the relevant competent departments improve and correct the problems exposed by the above inspections, and for those who have committed minor errors, they are ordered to reflect and correct, and for those who have committed dereliction of duty, they are punished according to discipline and law. But in the past two years, the supervisory organs at all levels still have many shortcomings in their work, and some problems have not been inspected in time, and some inspections have not been handled in time; some complex problems have not been inspected deeply and thoroughly, and sometimes events caused by the sabotage of bad elements are simply regarded as general events of lax institutions, bureaucratic leadership, and irresponsibility of workers, and therefore the problems cannot be thoroughly solved, the bad elements cannot receive the punishment they deserve, and valuable experience and lessons cannot be learned to educate the broad cadres and masses. These shortcomings should be corrected in the future.

To adapt to the requirements of the new stage of class struggle and more effectively oppose bad people and bad deeds to ensure the smooth progress of socialist construction, it is necessary to further strengthen state supervision, fully play the role of supervision, improve the ideological and combative nature of supervision, and under the leadership of the party committees and governments at all levels and with the assistance and support of relevant departments, rely on the broad masses to concentrate on supervising and inspecting the implementation of the economic construction plan, especially the industrial construction plan. To this end, the political, theoretical, and professional level of supervisory workers must be continuously improved, so that they have a clear and firm class stance, sharp political sensitivity, a high sense of responsibility, and a spirit of seeking truth from facts, and can resolutely fight against bourgeois ideology and saboteurs; can resolutely fight against bureaucracy, extravagance and waste, embezzlement and theft, and lawlessness and disorder, to consolidate state discipline and ensure the implementation of the first five-year plan.

**Speech by Representative Wang Renhe**

I fully agree with the first five-year plan for the development of the national economy of the People's Republic of China and the report by Vice Premier Li Fuquan on the development of the national economy's first five-year plan, and I fully agree with the report by Vice Premier Li Xiannian on the 1954 national budget and the 1955 national budget.

The five-year plan is a great program for the struggle of the whole country. We know that the figures stipulated in the five-year plan have such great significance: the first grand bridge will be built on the Yangtze River; a huge hydropower station will be established on the Yellow River; huge steel and iron combined enterprises will be built in Wuhan and Baotou; many wastelands will be reclaimed into fertile fields; we will manufacture airplanes, automobiles, tractors, locomotive engines, and various mechanical equipment by ourselves. Just as Lenin instructed, we will transition from the horse of poor peasants to the horse of huge mechanical industry. For such a great cause, our people will not hesitate to give their blood and sweat and energy. Our country is becoming more and more prosperous and strong; our people's lives are improving every year. We are very happy with the progress of socialist construction; but domestic and foreign enemies are not happy. The enemy is hostile to our cause, and their sabotage activities are crazy and cunning. At the beginning of our liberation, American imperialism and other enemies of the Chinese people had placed their hopes on the crazy idea that the new China would not be able to handle its economy and collapse. But the Communist Party of China and Chairman Mao led us to carry out three years of economic recovery work. By 1952, our national economy had largely recovered to the highest level before the war, and some industrial sectors had even greatly exceeded it; starting from 1953, we began to implement our first five-year plan for construction. After more than two years of practice, we are now able to formulate the plan more realistically and confidently based on reality, and raise some important industrial production to a higher level. History has determined that the people will inevitably win, and what power do the imperialists and all enemies of the Chinese people have to stop the progress of history?

On the other hand, every victory of socialist construction in our country is heartily congratulated by our brother countries and all peace-loving people in the world, because our victory is also their victory; and in the process of implementing the first five-year plan for construction in our country, the active support of the Soviet Union and various people's democratic countries has also become one of the factors for our victory. We should, with the sincerest feelings, thank the Soviet Union, because it is the experience of socialist construction in the Soviet Union that has enabled us to take fewer detours in our construction. With the long-term selfless help of the Soviet Union, we can more confidently complete and overfulfill our construction plan.

The 1954 national budget and the 1955 national budget are in line with our country's great economic construction plan. They have prepared the construction funds for us in a reasonable manner according to our construction steps and stipulated the reasonable expenditure. The 1955 budget clearly indicates the relationship between every unit of income and expenditure and every unit of labor and our national economic construction, and also clearly indicates the direction of our efforts. Completing the state budget is a step forward in the realization of our national economic plan.

In the report on the first five-year plan and the national budget and expenditure report, the issue of increasing production and practicing thrift is specially raised, which is very correct. The huge construction funds needed for socialist construction can only be accumulated from increasing production and saving. However, from past inspections, some funds have been wasted, which is unacceptable. I fully support Vice Premier Li Xiannian's opinion on punishing the behavior of embezzlement and waste. Again, in the 1955 budget, the expenditure for economic construction and social welfare is more than 75%, which strongly proves our country's sincere desire for peace. The slander and defamation of imperialists and all counter-revolutionaries are self-defeating. Finally, I would like to mention a couple of thoughts from my inspection before this meeting: First, after the release of the report on the first five-year plan for the development of the national economy, I heard that some people doubted the increase of grain production in the agricultural sector by only 17.6% compared to 1952. They said that the population growth rate in our country is quite high, and the current grain supply situation is much less than the average rate of rich countries. Therefore, in the first five-year plan, the improvement of the lives of the vast majority of farmers is still very little. I think this view is wrong. Because the characteristic of the first five-year plan for agriculture in our country is to implement the policy of "organizing together." The first five-year plan stipulates that the number of households participating in cooperatives reaches one-third, and further develops and improves various specific forms of labor mutual aid organizations. I myself have inspected the state-owned Nankou Farm and Huangtugang Township Agricultural Production Cooperative near Beijing, and from there, I learned that the income of agricultural production cooperatives is about twice that of when they were still in mutual aid groups, and the income of state-owned farms is about 70% higher than that of cooperatives due to the use of machinery. These two agricultural organizations are still very young and have some shortcomings, but after improvement, they will have greater improvements. This shows that only by gradually bringing agriculture into socialist organizations and implementing agricultural mechanization can income be increased and the lives of farmers be improved. Again, in the first five-year plan, the total value of agriculture and its sideline industries increased by 23.3%, which is not without important significance for improving the lives of farmers. Second, many representatives mentioned the sabotage activities of counter-revolutionaries during the group discussions, which is indeed a serious fact; in coastal areas such as Guangdong Province, because it is adjacent to Hong Kong and Macau, there are more cases of infiltration by American and Kuomintang spies and hidden counter-revolutionaries. During my inspection of the Qinghe Farm labor reform work, I also heard that there was a plot by a former Military Intelligence Bureau spy to organize a riot last year. Combined with the Pan Hannan and Hu Feng incidents, we deeply realize that the sabotage of the enemy is very cunning, and we cannot be complacent. To ensure that our socialist construction is not sabotaged, we must severely suppress all counter-revolutionaries and at the same time strengthen the study of Marxism-Leninism to enhance political vigilance.

I am fully satisfied with the work of the Standing Committee over the past year. The comprehensive plan for controlling and developing the Yellow River, which is valid for fifty years, is a rare giant project in the world. It will transform the river, which is famous for its disasters, to serve the interests of the people. This is something that can only happen in the era of Mao Zedong. I fully support this great plan. I propose that we pass the first five-year plan for the development of the national economy, the 1954 national budget and the 1955 national budget, the Military Service Law of the People's Republic of China, the work report of the Standing Committee, and the comprehensive plan for controlling and developing the Yellow River.

<h3>File continued from previous part</h3>

Title: Reports from the First Session of the First National People's Congress
Author:
Date: 1955-04-24
Page: 1

Xinhua News Agency, Beijing, April 24th.

In places like Huangmei County's Fusheng Township, where the leadership has been usurped by counter-revolutionaries or reactionary forces, this is not an isolated incident. These places have become strongholds for counter-revolutionary activities. Incidents such as "miracle water," "fairy goddesses," riots, banditry, forcing poor tenants to commit suicide, and murdering cadres often occur in these areas. Even in relatively good townships, some natural villages are often controlled by counter-revolutionaries or reactionary elements. To ensure the smooth progress of the socialist transformation of agriculture and the development of agricultural production, it is necessary to resolutely strike the enemy several more times. Strong work teams must be sent to backward townships and villages to mobilize the masses deeply and combine the transformation of backward townships with the suppression of counter-revolutionaries. When selecting township and village cadres, we must pay attention to selecting those with pure class backgrounds, clean histories, socialist ideological awareness, active work, firm struggle, and strong ties with the masses; we must not be deceived by disguised counter-revolutionaries or bad elements. Counter-revolutionary element Liu Zhensheng instructed Zhang Muxiang, saying: "You can delay the work, I'll take responsibility. My affairs you know, when the time comes to change the world, I'll take responsibility." Their specific methods are that Zhang Muxiang holds a meeting, and Liu Zhensheng's "mutual aid group" gives him ten points of work. Remnant counter-revolutionaries and some reactionary landlords and rich peasants are using various methods to infiltrate party organizations, government organizations, and mutual aid and cooperative organizations in the countryside. In some places, they have already infiltrated; others use the method of "pulling them over." Some counter-revolutionaries and reactionary landlords and rich peasants let their wives, daughters, and cadres have illicit relationships or marry, give gifts, send money to bribe and corrupt cadres. Money and women are dangerous weapons used by the enemy to attack us. We must strengthen the political and ideological education of district and township cadres, raise class vigilance, purify and strengthen the party organization, and smash the enemy's plots to consolidate the people's democratic dictatorship.

We know that on our road to progress, we will inevitably encounter many difficulties. The enemies of society and natural disasters are two sources of difficulties, and another source is the subjectivism, bureaucracy, and complacency in our work. These errors often give the enemy an advantage and create difficulties for ourselves. As long as we eliminate subjectivism, bureaucracy, and complacency, raise our political awareness, and better mobilize and unite the people to fight, all difficulties will be overcome, and the enemy's plots will be smashed. Under the wise leadership of the Communist Party of China and Chairman Mao, the first five-year plan of our country will definitely be completed, and we will strive to complete it ahead of schedule and over-fulfill it. The torrent of socialist revolution will sweep away all obstacles and destroy all decaying forces. Our people will definitely build a beautiful and happy life for themselves.

Xu Jie, Vice Minister, spoke:
I fully agree with and support Vice Premier Li Fuchun's report on the development of the national economy's first five-year plan and Vice Premier Li Xiannian's report on the 1954 national budget and the 1955 national budget.

In the development of the national economy's first five-year plan, geological work, in addition to providing the necessary mineral resources for the first five-year plan, must also prepare for the needs of the second five-year plan, and in some mineral aspects, it is necessary to consider the needs of the third five-year plan. Therefore, our geological work needs to be doubled. In terms of the percentage of geological exploration work done by the Geological Department in each year of the first five-year plan, if the total geological exploration work done in 1952 is taken as 100, then the total work done in the last year of the first five-year plan, 1957, would be 3,860, with an average annual increase of 108 percent. In simple terms, this means that the work volume should double each year. Our geological work must advance at this speed and continuously improve the quality of work in the process to meet the requirements of national economic construction.

In the first two years of the five-year plan, 1953 and 1954, the Geological Department's exploration work in submitting mineral reserves has basically completed the planned tasks for those two years; in iron, manganese, copper, lead, tin, and coal, which are the main mineral types, considerable reserves have been discovered, providing the necessary mineral raw materials and fuels for the country's steel enterprises, and establishing a new and huge mineral raw material base in non-ferrous metals. In addition to mineral exploration, in 1954, large-scale mineral surveys were organized, and some coal, chromium, molybdenum, lead, and copper minerals were found. In the two years, important river basin geological surveys and geological surveys for various water conservancy projects were also carried out, providing the necessary geological data for the design of the country's major construction projects.

The achievements of the first two years of the five-year plan are worth our satisfaction, but we must not be complacent. As mentioned earlier, to adapt to the rapid development of national construction, our annual planned work volume must double compared to the previous year. Therefore, the tasks of the last three years of the five-year plan, 1955 to 1957, are more arduous. Currently, the important mineral areas under exploration will be completed one after another, and a large number of new backup mineral areas must be found to ensure the continuous increase of mineral reserves. Coal, iron, manganese, copper, lead, and other minerals, in addition to continuing to increase reserves, must also establish new mineral raw material bases for the reasonable distribution of industrial enterprises. As for the black metals, non-ferrous metals, and other minerals necessary for industry, as well as diamonds, asbestos, etc., and phosphates, potash, etc., necessary for agriculture, some work has been done very little, and some have not yet started work, and it is necessary to actively organize forces, strengthen work, and quickly obtain reserves. The resource exploration work for natural oil and synthetic oil, undertaken by the Geological Department, has just begun and urgently needs to be strengthened. These major tasks require us to redouble our efforts in the future to complete them.

To better complete our tasks, we must vigorously solve the main problems existing at present and correct the shortcomings and errors in the work, among which the most important are the following:

First, the various links of geological work cannot adapt to each other. The mineral survey work, which is the vanguard of exploration, still cannot adapt to the progress of exploration, and thus cannot provide backup mineral areas for exploration in a timely manner. A large number of mass-reported minerals and known locations have not been widely checked, and at the same time, the regional geological surveys, which are the vanguard of surveys, have not been carried out on a large scale, resulting in mineral surveys lacking reliable geological bases and affecting the progress of surveys; large-scale and topographic surveys are far behind the needs of surveys and regional geological surveys. The situation where the various links of work do not adapt to each other will certainly seriously affect the progress and quality of work.

Second, the economic accounting perspective and planning perspective are weak, management work is not strict, and waste is serious. First of all, the various technical specifications and technical economic quotas are currently not complete and unified, and the execution of the existing specifications and quotas is not serious enough, exploration designs are not comprehensive, sometimes violate procedures, and cause rework waste; some drilling work blindly pursues quantity and neglects quality, resulting in scrapping. The design budget system, financial supervision, technical management, and production responsibility system are just beginning to be established and need to be vigorously implemented. The organization of labor and wage system still has unreasonable phenomena, and therefore the labor productivity has not been improved as expected. Basic construction has a tendency to extravagance and waste, and even some field work teams have the idea of "keeping up with the city" for temporary buildings.

Third, the learning of advanced Soviet science and experience is not enough, the technical and theoretical level is not high, and scientific research work has not been vigorously carried out, and it has not been able to play the guiding role for surveys and exploration work. In the past few years, under the enthusiastic help of Soviet experts, the work level has generally improved; but due to the lack of comprehensive and systematic learning of advanced Soviet experience, our current technical level and theoretical level still cannot meet the increasing requirements of national construction.

Fourth, political and ideological work is weak. The ideological education of a large number of workers and technical personnel has not been deepened, the resourceful individualist thought style has not been strictly criticized and corrected; subjectivism and various idealist thoughts have not been fully exposed and criticized, affecting the progress of various work and the improvement of work level.

To improve the work, we must take the following measures to address the above-mentioned shortcomings in the work:

First, in addition to continuing to expand the periphery of the existing exploration areas as much as possible, we must vigorously carry out systematic mineral surveys and inspections nationwide, mobilize the masses to report minerals, and fully mobilize the forces of various provincial industrial departments and geological surveys to quickly discover a large number of oil, iron, coal, lead, phosphate, and various metal and non-metal mineral areas, and carry out exploration work to ensure the continuous increase of mineral reserves. To enable the survey work to be carried out smoothly, we must accelerate the development of regional geological surveys and large-scale and topographic surveys. At the same time, we must strengthen geophysical prospecting and engineering geology and hydrology work to make various work adapt to each other.

Second, we must vigorously carry out scientific research work, comprehensively sort out and analyze the accumulated data, combine field surveys, and seriously study the types, mineralization, and distribution laws of various minerals to play the guiding role of scientific research work for mineral surveys and exploration work.

Third, implement the policy of increasing production and practicing economy, further formulate and revise various technical specifications and technical economic quotas, improve the organization of labor and wage system, strengthen the design budget and economic accounting system, strictly implement financial supervision, and improve the level of management work.

Fourth, to further strengthen the geological work team, we must strengthen school education and the training of cadres in the work. At the same time, we must continue to strengthen the learning of advanced Soviet science and technology by cadres in office, and adopt methods such as cadre training classes, part-time study, and work summaries to improve professional level.

Fifth, we must seriously strengthen political and ideological work, criticize various bourgeois thought styles, establish a dialectical materialist scientific work attitude among cadres, especially among technical personnel, improve the political vigilance of cadres, and prevent the sabotage of hidden counter-revolutionaries. On the vast territory of our motherland, the geological conditions for the formation of various mineral deposits are fully present. All geological conditions for the formation of sedimentary, magmatic, and metamorphic deposits, such as the complete development of various geological age strata, various types of igneous rock bodies representing various geological age magmatic activities and crustal movements, and various geological structural forms, are widely distributed in our country. In fact, from the known mineral areas in the country, various types of metal and non-metal mineral deposits have also been found in our country. All these indicate that the mineral resources of our country are rich. Take oil as an example. In the western and southwestern regions of our country, there are vast basins, where oil seeps and layers and geological structures suitable for oil production and storage have been found everywhere; the North China Plain and the Songliao Plain in Northeast China have also found oil seeps. Although oil geology is very complex, we believe that with continued efforts in this area, we will definitely find more and larger oil-producing areas in our country. In short, the exploration work in the past few years has discovered huge mineral reserves; continued efforts in the future will open up a broader prospect for the mineral resources of our country. Under the correct leadership of the Communist Party of China and the State Council and the support of the people of the whole country and the enthusiastic help of Soviet experts, through the unremitting efforts of all geological workers, the socialist industrialization of our country will be able to obtain powerful guarantees in terms of mineral resources.

Le Songsheng, Representative, spoke:
I fully support Vice Premier Li Fuchun's report on the development of the national economy's first five-year plan, Vice Premier Li Xiannian's report on the 1954 national budget and the 1955 national budget, Vice Premier Peng Dehuai's report on the draft of the Law on National Service of the People's Republic of China, and Vice Chairman Peng Zhen's report on the work of the Standing Committee of the National People's Congress. The formulation of the first five-year plan for the development of the national economy is an unprecedented event in our country's history. The implementation of the national economic development plan with socialist industrialization as the center is a major step to achieve the country's transitional period's overall task. Its goal is to build our country into a prosperous and strong socialist society after several five-year plans. This is the unanimous wish and demand of the people of the whole country. Only under the leadership of the Communist Party of China and Chairman Mao in the new China can we have the possibility of realizing this great plan.

The socialist transformation of capitalist industry and commerce is an important part of the implementation of the first five-year plan. Only by restricting the blind and destructive nature of capitalist economy and gradually bringing it into the national planning track can we develop the national economy according to the laws of socialist economy in a planned and proportional manner. In recent years, under the leadership of the Party and the government, Beijing has implemented the policy of utilizing, restricting, and transforming capitalist industry and commerce, and the work of socialist transformation has achieved remarkable results. In the industrial sector, the number of public-private joint ventures increased from 9 in 1953 to 32 in 1954, and the proportion of their output value in the total industrial output value of the city increased from 3.3% to 4.96%. In 1954, the total value of the state's processing orders, purchases, and sales for private industry accounted for 71% of the total output value of private industry, up from 58.5% in 1953. Public-private joint ventures, with the socialist component in a leading position within the enterprise, have improved the enthusiasm of workers, and generally improved technology, increased varieties, improved quality, production, management, and reduced costs in various aspects. More and more people have seen the superiority of public-private joint ventures and are actively creating conditions to strive for this bright future. To improve the backwardness of private industry, in 1954, under the leadership of the government and the assistance of workers, an increase in production and reduction in waste campaign was launched in more than 300 private factories, which achieved remarkable results in improving quality, reducing costs, saving raw materials, and completing state processing orders on time, in quantity, and in quality. For example, in the city's 49 private weaving factories, after the increase in production and reduction in waste campaign was launched for more than a month, the output of grade-A products increased by 5.6%, and the number of factories that could meet the company's quality standards increased from 3 to 20, increasing the confidence of the capitalists in management. This spring, the government, according to the central government's instructions on comprehensive and balanced arrangements, arranged the production and management of private industry, helped solve the supply problems of more than 80 kinds of raw materials, adjusted the profits of 85 kinds of products, increased tasks, and improved the inspection procedures of finished products. After these measures, the production of private industry has been basically maintained, and there has been a certain profit. In the commercial sector, at the beginning of 1954, about 700 private wholesalers dealing with major commodities could no longer continue their operations due to significant changes in the market. The government, according to their requests, made proper arrangements; since 1953, the state has successively implemented the unified purchase and sale of grain, oil, and cotton cloth. Most of the private retailers in these industries have been entrusted by the state to sell or consign, and have been brought into the track of state capitalism; at the same time, other retailers have been gradually brought into the track of state capitalism in various forms such as consignment, agency, batch purchase and retail, and agency wholesale. By October 1954, 23% of the total number of private retailers in the city had been brought into the track of state capitalism. These "consignment" and "agency" private commercial enterprises, because they have been brought into the track of national economic planning, have been able to solve the problems of supply and sales channels appropriately, and the business situation is relatively stable. This spring, various relevant state-owned companies have given appropriate consideration to the supply and business volume of private commerce, implemented the policy of comprehensive and balanced arrangements, and turned around the loss-making phenomenon of some private commerce. To improve the various shortcomings of private commerce, last winter, a campaign to improve management was launched in 700 private commercial enterprises in the city, reducing waste, establishing necessary systems, and preparing for consignment and agency. Currently, the work of improving management is being further carried out in larger private commercial enterprises, with the main content being to reduce the circulation cost of commodities, follow the state plan, and change the management style.

In the process of the state's socialist transformation of capitalist industry and commerce, as Vice Premier Li Fuchun pointed out in his report: "There are still some capitalists who take a negative attitude towards socialist transformation. Some of them are still carrying out 'acts harmful to public interests, disrupting social economic order, and sabotaging national economic plans' prohibited by the constitution, using more cunning methods to commit 'five poisons'; some even resist or sabotage socialist transformation. Such people should be subject to public condemnation and legal punishment." We must seriously fight against these law-breaking capitalists, call on patriotic industrialists and businessmen to draw a clear line between law-abiding and law-breaking, expose and report their illegal acts, and request the government to punish them according to law.

To ensure the realization of the first five-year plan for the development of the national economy, private industrialists and businessmen must sincerely accept socialist transformation, love the country and the law, actively manage, study hard, and gradually walk onto various forms of state capitalism tracks; and should deeply realize that the more successful the socialist construction and socialist transformation, the more the imperialists and all counter-revolutionaries will try every means to sabotage our construction. As in the recent exposure of the counter-revolutionary activities of the Pan Hannian and Hu Feng groups, they are our enemies. Therefore, we private industrialists and businessmen should unite closely around the Communist Party of China, transform our thoughts, actively participate in the struggle to smash all hidden counter-revolutionaries, increase vigilance, overcome passivity, and not give the enemy any opportunity; increase production, practice economy, and strive for the sincere acceptance of socialist transformation and the elimination of all counter-revolutionaries and opposition to domestic and foreign enemies!

Finally, I am very excited about Vice Premier Deng Zihui's report on the comprehensive plan for the treatment of the Yellow River's water disasters and the development of the Yellow River's water resources. Hearing about the greatness and difficulty of this plan and the magnificent and beautiful prospect of comprehensive utilization, I once again deeply feel that in the era of people's democracy under Mao Zedong, it is an era of turning human ideals into reality. Due to the treatment and utilization of the Yellow River, the progress of socialist construction will be greatly promoted, benefiting human society and future generations, and changing the appearance of our great motherland. I cheer for this unprecedented great construction!

Tao Luba, Representative, spoke:
I fully agree with the reports made by Vice Premiers Li Fuchun, Li Xiannian, Peng Dehuai, and Deng Zihui, and Vice Chairman Peng Zhen to the meeting.

I think the speed of industrial development set by the first five-year plan in our country is correct, and I feel very encouraged. Everyone knows that "developing agriculture is the basic condition for ensuring the development of industry and the completion of the overall economic plan." Now I would like to express some opinions on this issue.

I think the production increase target set for agriculture in the five-year plan is active and reliable, and it is compatible with the needs of industrial development. The investment in agriculture and the measures taken in the plan are also appropriate. Of course, to complete the agricultural production increase plan, we must make great efforts. It is wrong to underestimate the difficulties and be blindly optimistic. However, some people lack confidence in agricultural production increase, and thus doubt the development of industry. This is groundless. Judging from the situation in Shanxi Province, the conditions for completing and even over-fulfilling the agricultural production increase plan are fully available. In recent years, despite the fact that the arable land area in Shanxi Province has not changed much, the situation of grain and cotton production increase is as follows: 1952 was a year of full harvest, with a total grain production of 7.6 billion jin, an increase of 20% over 1951. The total cotton production reached 180 million jin, an increase of 67% over 1951; in 1953, the total grain production increased by 12% over 1952, but the total cotton production decreased by 15% due to the reduction of planting area, but the yield per unit area increased by 3%; in 1954, although about one-sixth of the arable land suffered serious disasters, the total grain production still increased by more than 7% over 1952 and by 29% over 1951; the total cotton production increased by 3% over 1952 and by 70% over 1951. If calculated by the total agricultural output value, 1954 increased by 13.6% over 1952. The above figures can fully illustrate that the potential of agricultural production is very great. Then, what methods have we used in the past few years to tap this potential? In summary, there are the following points: First, vigorously develop the mutual aid and cooperation movement. In 1952, the entire province had only 546 agricultural production cooperatives, with participating households accounting for 0.4% of the total number of households, and households participating in mutual aid groups accounting for about 50%. By this year, the entire province has more than 31,000 cooperatives, with cooperative households accounting for 41% of the total number of households, and households participating in mutual aid groups accounting for 76% of the total number of households. There are 16 counties that have basically achieved cooperation. Experience has proven that where cooperation is correctly developed, the effect on agricultural production increase is the most significant. For example, in Huguang County, 66.4% of the total number of households have joined cooperatives, and in 1954, the total grain production of the county increased by 18.5% over the bumper harvest year of 1952. Second, change the cultivation system, expand the replanting area, and carry out land basic construction to turn wasteland into good land. As a result, in 1954, the total crop planting area in the entire province increased by 1 million mu over 1952 and by 7.8 million mu over 1951. Third, carry out water and soil conservation and small water conservancy projects in a planned manner. In 1954, the total area of paddy fields and irrigated land in the entire province reached 6.82 million mu, an increase of 2.9 million mu over 1952. Fourth, since 1952, we have systematically summarized and promoted various high-yield experiences of crops, such as the use of new agricultural tools, improvement of cultivation techniques, expansion of the planting area of superior varieties and high-yield crops, promotion of rational dense planting and intercropping, and the launch of mass fertilizer movements, all of which have achieved great results. For example, cotton planting, due to the promotion of the advanced experience of labor model Qu Yao Li, the yield per unit area in the Jinan cotton-producing area has increased year by year since 1952, reaching 53 jin of raw cotton per mu in 1954, up from 39 jin in 1951. The county of Quwo in the Jinan area has reached 65 jin. Fifth, develop diversified economy, and promote the experience of combining agriculture, forestry, animal husbandry, and water conservancy in Baisha Zhujiang Village and Yangjiaoping Village. In Shanxi Province, where more than 70% of the total area is mountainous, this is an important way to increase farmers' income and achieve agricultural production increase. The above methods have proven to be effective in practice. The problem is that so far, each method we have done is very insufficient, and there are still many shortcomings in the work we have done. But this shows that the potential for agricultural production increase is still very great. As long as we implement these methods better, plus the state's investment in agriculture and technical assistance, if there are no unexpected serious disasters, we believe that it is completely possible to strive for over-fulfilling the agricultural production increase plan.

Those who lack confidence in agricultural production increase often exaggerate the shortcomings of the grain unified purchase and sale work, and thus doubt and oppose the grain unified purchase and sale policy. On this issue, I fully agree with Vice Premier Chen Yun's speech. Judging from the situation in Shanxi Province, in the past two years, due to the increase in grain production, in addition to meeting the needs of Shanxi Province, more than 5 billion jin of grain can be exported each year. This year, in May, the grain supply in some rural areas of Shanxi Province also experienced a tense situation for a while. What is the actual situation? What are the reasons? This is a problem that needs to be clarified. In late May, when the work of rectifying the unified purchase and sale in the entire province ended, we organized more than 900 party and non-party cadres to conduct a one-month investigation in 300 townships. According to the materials from these 300 townships, it is shown that the originally identified surplus households totaled 50,360, of which 3% were not supposed to be purchased but were purchased, and 9% were supposed to be purchased less but were purchased more, totaling 12%; 5% were supposed to be purchased more but were purchased less. 83% were completely reasonable. In addition, there were actually surplus households that were not identified as surplus households, accounting for about 4% of the total number of households in the 300 townships. In the 300 townships, the originally identified shortage households totaled 30,800, of which 12% were not supposed to be supplied but were supplied, 18% were supposed to be supplied less but were supplied more, 12% were supposed to be supplied more but were supplied less, and 58% were supplied reasonably. In addition, there were actually shortage households that were not identified as shortage households, accounting for about 3% of the total number of households in the 300 townships. After the rectification, the supply became reasonable, and the number of shortage households decreased by 20%, and the grain unified purchase and sale volume decreased by 23%. The above materials show that although the grain unified purchase and sale work in the past period had many problems, it was generally correct. The tense situation that once appeared in some rural areas was not caused by the state's purchase and sale indicators being too low, nor was it caused by the grain unified purchase and sale policy not being acceptable to the majority of farmers. The reasons are: on the one hand, due to the shortcomings in our work. This is mainly due to the poor understanding of the situation, the tasks arranged are not very realistic, the implementation of the policy is not deep enough, the inspection work and the correction of deviations are not timely, especially the failure to seriously pay attention to the demarcation of surplus households, self-sufficient households, and shortage households, and the demarcation of full shortage, half shortage, less shortage, and slight shortage among shortage households. The facts have proven that in 20-plus counties in Shanxi Province, due to the good work, there was basically no such tense situation. On the other hand, more importantly, some surplus households, under the influence of rich peasant thoughts and grain speculators, appeared as so-called "thought shortage households," and they were afraid of being identified as surplus households and shouted for shortage; coupled with the landlords, counter-revolutionaries, and other bad elements taking the opportunity to spread rumors and sabotage, causing trouble. In this situation, some rural leading cadres were not sober-minded, did not distinguish between true and false shortage households and enemy lines, but blindly adopted the wrong method of supplying whoever shouted the loudest; as a result, the more grain was supplied, the more people shouted for shortage, and the bad elements thought there was an opportunity to take advantage of, so their attacks became more rampant. Therefore, in the rectification of the grain unified purchase and sale work, we first criticized the rightist wavering sentiment among cadres, resolutely corrected the shortcomings in the work, and at the same time severely struck the sabotage activities of counter-revolutionaries. The facts have proven that by doing this, not only the grain unified purchase and sale indicators were greatly reduced, but also the majority of farmers further clarified the benefits of the unified purchase and sale policy, and improved revolutionary vigilance, which in turn promoted the high tide of mutual aid and cooperation and the increase in production and reduction in waste movement.

The grain unified purchase and sale work is a new work, and we still lack sufficient experience. The State Council and the Central Committee's instructions on implementing the "three-definite" policy for grain have been actively supported by the majority of farmers. Of course, there will still be some deviations and problems in the future work, but if this is used to exaggerate the shortcomings in the work and doubt the grain unified purchase and sale policy, it would be completely wrong. Take an example: in April this year, due to the fact that the leading cadres of Pingyao County in Shanxi Province heard that many people were shouting for shortage and "lost their composure," the County People's Committee issued a wrong notice, stipulating that in the entire county, farmers could exchange grain, seeds, and feed for each other, and any township or individual should not interfere. After this notice was issued, the "black market" flooded in just 7-8 days, and grain prices soared, causing widespread dissatisfaction among local farmers. For example, farmer Liang Jutong said to himself while grinding flour: "Chairman Mao, will the grain unified purchase and sale policy change? It seems that the cadres below have made a mistake." Only the rich peasants and grain speculators were happy, and they smiled to people, saying: "The grain market has been liberated." The chaotic and tense situation caused by this was quickly turned around after we realized and immediately corrected it. It is obvious that this proves that doubting the grain unified purchase and sale policy and attempting to return to capitalist free trade is only beneficial to the free spread of capitalism in cities and rural areas, but it is harmful and of no benefit to the majority of farmers. Therefore, we must resolutely implement the grain unified purchase and sale policy and not waver at all. Vice Premier Li Fuchun pointed out in his report that the five advantages of the grain unified purchase and sale policy are completely in line with the actual situation, and we should vigorously publicize them.

Now, the imperialists, who hate the industrialization of our country, are pinning their hopes on the failure of our agriculture. However, the facts have proven and will continue to prove that the failure is not ours but theirs. Some people, due to their lack of confidence in agricultural production increase, want to use the method of reducing the speed of industrialization to develop agriculture. Obviously, this idea is completely contrary to the common wishes and actual situation of the people of our country. Therefore, we must oppose it.

This meeting, we heard Vice Premier Deng Zihui's report on the comprehensive plan for the treatment of the Yellow River's water disasters and the development of the Yellow River's water resources, and we feel very happy. The wish of the Chinese people for thousands of years to treat the water disasters of the Yellow River and the beautiful vision of developing the Yellow River's water resources have finally come true in the era of Mao Zedong. This great creation has further strengthened our confidence in the development of industry and agriculture. Undoubtedly, the people of Shanxi Province will, together with the people of other provinces along the Yellow River, fully shoulder their responsibilities according to the requirements of this plan. The practice of farmers in the mountainous areas of Shanxi Province has proven that water and soil conservation is not only a fundamental measure for the treatment of the Yellow River but also the key link for the increase in agricultural production in the mountainous areas. Therefore, last August, the People's Congress of Shanxi Province passed a resolution on the comprehensive development of water and soil conservation work and formulated a 15-year plan. This year, special agencies have been established in 22 counties, and a large number of full-time cadres have been sent to carry out this work comprehensively. We are convinced that the great plan of comprehensive utilization of the Yellow River will be warmly supported and actively supported by millions of laboring people. Therefore, it will definitely succeed.

The first five-year plan, with the development of heavy industry as the center, is a program of historic significance for the construction of socialism in our country. It vividly shows us the increasingly prosperous country and the increasingly improved living standards of the people. Let us unite and, under the leadership of the Communist Party of China and Chairman Mao Zedong, work hard, overcome difficulties, increase production, practice economy, and strive with confidence to complete and over-fulfill the first five-year plan. Gu Daicun, Representative, spoke:
I fully support the draft of the first five-year plan for the development of the national economy of the People's Republic of China, the draft of the Law on National Service, Vice Premier Li Fuchun's report on the first five-year plan for the development of the national economy, and the reports of Vice Premiers Li Xiannian, Peng Dehuai, and Deng Zihui, as well as Vice Chairman Peng Zhen. I suggest that the meeting approve them and call on the people of the whole country to resolutely fight for the completion of the first five-year plan of our country, the implementation of the state budget, the implementation of the Law on National Service, and the realization of the great plan to treat the water disasters of the Yellow River and develop the water resources of the Yellow River.

The main task of Guangdong in the first five-year plan period is to vigorously develop agricultural production with mutual aid and cooperation as the center, and at the same time, actively and plannedly develop local industries, and strengthen the socialist transformation of capitalist industry and commerce and individual handicrafts, to serve the country's socialist industrialization overall task.

Under the care and strong support of the central government, through the hard work of the people of the whole province, after the completion of land reform in the whole province, especially after the strengthening of the leadership of agricultural production by the local party committees and various levels of state organs, the mutual aid and cooperation movement in agricultural production has been developed, and there has been significant development. In 1952, the total grain production reached 17.9 billion jin, exceeding the highest annual production before the war by 8%; in 1953, Guangdong's agricultural production achieved a comprehensive and bumper harvest; in 1954, due to the severe frost disaster that had not been seen in decades, the production of coarse grains was seriously reduced, but the production of rice still increased. This has fundamentally changed the grain situation in Guangdong compared to before liberation. Guangdong is no longer a grain-deficient province, but can also export a certain amount of grain to support the country's socialist industrialization. The people of the whole province, especially the 700 million people in cities, industrial areas, economic crop areas, and fishery and salt areas, whether during the new grain season or during the lean period, can guarantee to obtain grain supplies at stable prices. The people of the whole province have gradually improved their lives on the basis of the development of industrial and agricultural production.

Guangdong is located in the subtropical zone, with high temperatures, sufficient rainfall, evergreen all year round, and three crops a year. These are favorable conditions for the development of agricultural production. However, uneven rainfall, severe pests, frequent typhoons, and various natural disasters have seriously threatened agricultural production increase. In just the second half of last year to the first half of this year, the entire province has been hit by water, drought, wind, pests, and frost disasters; especially last winter's severe cold, even Hainan Island froze; this spring's severe drought, after the summer solstice, there were still many paddy fields that could not be plowed. These are disasters that have not been seen in decades, resulting in the severe loss of winter crops and almost no spring plowing. Of course, disasters will increase our difficulties, but they will not make us surrender. Under the leadership of the Communist Party and the people's government, with 13,000 agricultural production cooperatives and 840,000 mutual aid groups as the core, we launched a large-scale anti-drought struggle. The People's Liberation Army stationed in Guangdong stopped training for a total of six days twice to help farmers fight against drought; more than 100,000 cadres, workers, students, and staff from state organs, institutions, enterprises, and schools in the entire province participated in the anti-drought struggle; and more than 6 million farmers directly participated in the anti-drought movement. This anti-drought production army persisted for three to four months and carried out tens of thousands of river-blocking, well-digging, spring-digging, and saltwater-repelling projects. From mid-March to early May, all large and small rivers in the province, except the West River, had water flow and were blocked. The province has a total of 21,400 river-blocking projects. The largest of these was the successful completion of the sealing of the Han River project in five days, which made the Han River water, for the first time in history, stop flowing south to the sea and instead flow west to irrigate the 760,000 mu of drought-affected paddy fields in the Pingjiang Plain. The province dug 353,000 wells in the eastern, central, and western regions of Guangdong alone, solving the problem of saving seedlings and transplanting for a large number of paddy fields. The province mobilized more than 250,000 dragon-bone carts and more than 1,000 horsepower of water pumps (including 1,000 horsepower of water pumps sent by Wuhan City, Hubei Province, to support), solving the water problem for a large number of dry fields in hilly areas. Farmers in the lower reaches of the Zhujiang, Hanjiang, Rongjiang, and Jianjiang rivers adopted methods such as "blocking springs and sealing holes" and "storing fresh water and resisting salt water" to overcome the threat of seawater backflow into fields. In this way, the people of the entire province finally overcame the severe drought, transplanted more than 90% of the paddy fields before the summer solstice, completed the spring plowing production task, and immediately strengthened field management, did a good job of fertilizer application, weeding, and reasonable irrigation and drainage. The areas with good water conservancy work in the Hanjiang Plain appeared to be bumper harvests. Now the entire province has entered the busy summer harvest season, and various places have suffered severe floods, with hundreds of thousands of mu of flooded fields and more than a million disaster-stricken people, causing heavy losses. In terms of the entire province, a reduction in production in the first crop is inevitable. We deeply realize that to develop Guangdong's agricultural production, we must overcome various natural disasters. This is a very arduous task for the people of the entire province of Guangdong.

In the anti-drought production, the organizational advantages of the entire province's mutual aid and cooperation organizations were fully demonstrated, proving that once farmers are organized, they are more likely to overcome natural disasters. As the representative of the National People's Congress, Mr. Wang Han Guo, led the agricultural production cooperative, although it also suffered from a severe drought disaster, but their cooperative increased production by 14.5% on the basis of the victory of the anti-drought struggle. This proves that we must develop agricultural production with the development of mutual aid and cooperation as the center, which is completely correct.

We fully support the state's policy of concentrating the main force on the development of heavy industry during the first five-year plan period. From the situation of agricultural production development in Guangdong Province in recent years, the target of increasing agricultural and sideline production by 23.3% within five years in the first five-year plan is also completely correct. The people of Guangdong will definitely strive to complete this task and even over-fulfill it.

Since the people of Guangdong want to develop agricultural production in the first five-year plan period to serve the country's overall task of socialist industrialization, in addition to strengthening the measures for the development of agricultural production from various aspects, it is also necessary to do a good job in the unified purchase and sale of grain. This is of great significance to the socialist construction of the state and the socialist transformation of agriculture. The implementation of the unified purchase and sale of grain not only kept the grain market in Guangdong stable, ensuring the stable life of the people of the entire province, but also enabled the people of the entire province to overcome the severe frost disaster and drought disaster that had not been seen in decades. Guangdong did experience a tense situation in grain supply for a while this year, causing work losses. However, this is not, as some people say, "the grain unified purchase and sale policy is bad, it does not take care of farmers and causes tension," nor is it, as some other people say, "Guangdong's grain has not increased, but the unified purchase and sale has taken away a large amount of grain from Guangdong farmers." It should be said that the main reason for the tense situation in Guangdong's grain supply this year is that we made deviations in the implementation of the central policy and did not do a good job in the unified purchase and sale work.

Due to the fact that the grain situation in the entire province of Guangdong has been very stable for several years, and the summer purchase task was completed smoothly last year, there was a certain degree of complacency in the thinking of the provincial leadership and various levels of cadres. The summer purchase was not tightened last year, and only 30.3% of the annual task was completed, while the summer sale was left to flow freely, and 3 billion jin more were sold. Nearly 70% of the annual purchase task was concentrated in the autumn to be completed, and at the same time, to support the disaster areas across the country, additional tasks were added, and the overall purchase task was a bit heavy. However, the winter crops also encountered a severe frost disaster that had not been seen in decades, with losses of sweet potatoes and wheat equivalent to 7-8 billion jin of rice, which made the food of some farmers really not enough. Coupled with the spring drought, farmers' psychology was tense, and they hoarded grain to prepare for disasters, so the tense situation of grain supply began to appear in January this year. Although the provincial leadership had discovered this problem at that time and greatly relaxed the sale indicators, due to the cadres' "emphasis on purchase and neglect of sale" mentality, the "less supply for less shortage, no supply for no shortage" policy was not seriously implemented, but an average approach was adopted, resulting in the grain sales in January, February, and March this year, although greatly exceeding the same period last year (in February this year, the sales exceeded the same period last year by 44.47%), the problem was still not well solved. In early April, the province, on the one hand, arranged for the rectification of the sale, and on the other hand, greatly reduced the sale, trying to reverse the phenomenon of serious oversale of grain, but due to the full participation of the entire province in the anti-drought production struggle, the rectification of the sale was actually not carried out, and various places still issued the reduced indicators evenly, so from mid-April to early June, the supply work in severely disaster-stricken areas such as Maoming, Taishan, and Yangjiang in western Guangdong, and in grain-producing areas such as eastern and northern Guangdong and some mountainous areas in Hainan was indeed very tense. This is the biggest mistake in our work. It was not until late May, when the anti-drought production in the entire province was basically completed, and early June, that we had the time to mobilize 16,000 cadres to go down to the countryside to do a good job in the "three-definite" work and further rectify the grain work. Now the grain situation in Guangdong has completely eased. At the same time, it must be pointed out that even in the extremely tense situation of grain supply at that time, according to the results of the "three-definite" work investigation, it was proved that only about 10% of the rural population really lacked grain and needed to be supplied, while about 90% of the people could basically get by or even had some surplus grain, and their shouting had a great deal of falseness.

From this, it can be seen that the state's grain unified purchase and sale policy is completely correct. As for the tense situation that appeared in Guangdong's grain sale for a while, it was caused by the mistakes and shortcomings in our work. If we had not had the phenomenon of "loose in the front and tight in the back" in the grain unified purchase and sale work last year, and had grasped the grain sale work tightly from January this year, and had not adopted the method of sudden reduction in sale (it can be affirmed that if the reduction in sale method had not been adopted in April, the most that would have been oversold would have been 1 billion jin of rice, which is bearable for Guangdong's current grain situation), then the tense situation in April and May could have been completely avoided. This is a very profound lesson for the entire province of Guangdong, and we have already corrected it in conjunction with the "three-definite" work. Judging from the current situation of the first batch of townships that have completed the "three-definite" work, we have the confidence to do a good job in the grain work. The grain unified purchase and sale policy is one of the fundamental measures of the state in the transitional period, and it cannot be shaken at all. As for the shortcomings and errors in our work, they must be corrected. The current rampant sabotage activities of counter-revolutionaries are worthy of our serious vigilance. We fully support the Standing Committee's decision to arrest and try the counter-revolutionaries Pan Hannian and Hu Feng. Guangdong is located on the front line of national defense, and the enemy situation is serious. The people of Guangdong, who are fighting day and night against open and hidden enemies, deeply understand the seriousness of strengthening national defense forces and strengthening the suppression of counter-revolutionaries. In the past year, due to our failure to grasp the work of suppressing counter-revolutionaries, counter-revolutionaries and various bad elements were very rampant, and the enemy's acts of murder, sabotage, rumor-mongering, and slander were endless. The proportion of criminal cases in Guangzhou City and other cities has increased significantly, seriously threatening the social order, economic construction, and the consolidation of national defense in the south of the motherland. Therefore, we must quickly correct the shortcomings in our work, unite the people of the entire province more closely, and resolutely fight against open and hidden counter-revolutionaries, eliminate them completely, consolidate the coastal and border defenses, and fight to the end for the smooth progress of the great cause of socialist construction in our great motherland!

Wang Guoxing, Representative, spoke:
During the meeting, I participated in the discussion of the draft of the first five-year plan for the development of the national economy of the People's Republic of China, which made me feel that its basic tasks and the center set by it, as well as the specific policies, methods, and steps for the implementation of the plan, are complete and feasible. Especially in the regulation of the progress of economic and cultural development and the training and allocation of construction personnel, it fully pays attention to the specific situation and characteristics of minority areas according to needs and possibilities, which creates important conditions for further improving the material and cultural life of the people of all ethnic groups in our country, making me feel excited and inspired. We, the Li and Miao people of Hainan, will never forget that before liberation, we suffered from the brutal oppression and exploitation of imperialism and the reactionary rule of the Kuomintang, and we could not even talk about industry. Even some handicraft products were brought in from other places through unequal exchange, and the entire region had no schools, almost illiterate, making us live in a state of hunger, poverty, and backwardness for a long time. Therefore, we once resisted and fought against the reactionary rule of the Kuomintang with great difficulty and tenacity, and finally, through the struggle, we found the correct leadership of the Communist Party of China, which enabled us to achieve complete liberation, establish a people's democratic government, and implement the system of ethnic regional autonomy. Now, we, the Li and Miao people of Hainan, and all other ethnic minorities in the country, have united and lived in the friendly and cooperative big family of our various ethnic peoples, which cannot be separated, and have gradually entered the overall track of the country's transitional period from the current development stage of the autonomous region, opening up a broad road to socialism for the future development of the Li and Miao people. Since the establishment of the Hainan Li and Miao Autonomous Region three years ago, there have been significant progress and development in politics, economy, and culture. According to the current actual needs and possible conditions, we have established power plants, oil presses, brick and tile factories, lime factories, printing factories, and grain, red and white vine processing factories, etc. In the development of agricultural production, we have implemented the socialist transformation of agriculture, gradually changing the extremely backward cultivation technology of slash-and-burn, wooden plows, and wooden harrows in the past. Many farmers have learned and adopted iron agricultural tools and pest control, and with the help of the government and the self-reliance of the masses, we have built or started to build a total of 8,266 large, medium, and small water conservancy projects, reducing various natural disasters such as wind, pests, water, and drought; coupled with the steady development of the mutual aid and cooperation movement, the entire region has established 129 agricultural cooperatives, and the counties of Changle and Lingao have organized 32,502 households, accounting for 59.7% of the total number of households in the two counties; making grain production increase year by year. For example, in 1954, the county of Qiongzhong increased production by 19.73%, and Baoting increased production by 20%. In terms of culture and health, by the end of 1954, there were 510 primary schools, 5 secondary schools, and cultural palaces, cultural stations, film teams, and ethnic song and dance troupes, from the autonomous prefecture to the county, district, and township, a total of 261 health centers, clinics, health stations, health stations, health stations, health stations, and health stations. From last year to this year, the entire region bought more than 10,000 oxen, and now all farmers in the entire region have clothes to wear, and in Baisha Zhujiang Township, Dongpai Village, every farmer has two sets of clothes, and most of them have cotton quilts, cotton blankets, and mosquito nets. This can be said that we, the Li and Miao people of Hainan, have begun to live a healthy, happy, free, and happy life under the correct leadership and great care and help of the Party and the government. This is the victory of the Communist Party of China and Chairman Mao's ethnic policy, and it is also the great achievement that has been preliminarily manifested in the minority areas in the country's transitional period development plan and the implementation of the first five-year plan.

Our Hainan Li and Miao Autonomous Region is located in the subtropical zone, with excellent natural conditions, and crops can be harvested three times a year. In mountainous areas, there are various mineral resources and special products suitable for industrial raw materials. Wuzhishan has rich forests, and coastal areas have excellent ports that can be developed, and the fishery and salt industry have a great development prospect. With these superior objective conditions, our confidence and determination to support the industrialization of the motherland have been further strengthened. But we will not only see the favorable conditions for national construction and ignore the existence of difficulties, nor should we be complacent about the achievements we have made. We must fully pay attention to the fact that the minority areas have been in a state of extreme backwardness due to the long-term historical legacy, and we must work hard to learn, improve our political, cultural, and technical levels, and adapt to the requirements of the motherland for us. At the same time, our Hainan Li and Miao Autonomous Region is located on the front line of national defense. When our country is carrying out large-scale economic construction, whether it is the open or hidden enemies from outside, such as the special agents of the United States and the Kuomintang, or the counter-revolutionaries hidden inside, they will definitely try every means to sabotage our people's happy cause. We must further strengthen the unity and friendship between ethnic groups and within ethnic groups, maintain high vigilance, and closely cooperate with the national defense army to give a powerful blow to all enemies who dare to invade and sabotage. Finally, I will do my best to unite all cadres, unite the Li and Miao people, continue to carry forward the spirit of patriotism, improve the enthusiasm and creativity of production, practice economy, increase production, and complete and over-fulfill the specific tasks assigned to us by the state plan on time, in quantity, and in quality, and strive for the complete realization of the first five-year plan.

Wazha Moji, Representative, spoke:
